isclaimer 

he Superior Court of California, County of Sacramento ("Court"), has prepared this 
Legal Glossary.  The Court cannot guarantee that the translations contained therein are 
completely accurate, although reasonable attempts were made to achieve this goal.  This 
glossary is to be used for general reference purposes only, should be considered a "work-
in-progress," and is not intended to provide legal advice.  This glossary is not intended to 
be used as a study guide for purposes of passing California court interpreter certification 
examinations, as some terminology might differ when used in specific context.  

Neither the Administrative Office of the Courts, nor the Superior Court of California, 
Sacramento County, nor any of its officials or employees assumes any legal liability or 
responsibility for the accuracy of these translations.  For more information or comments, 
please contact Ms. Elaine Flores, Administrative Services Officer II of the Court, at (916) 
874-8663 or via e-mail at florese@saccourt.com.

DICTIONAR DE TERMENI JURIDICI 

   

1203.03 PC MOTION – Request to cancel, modify, change or terminate probation. 

OTIUNEA PC 1203.03 – Cererea de anulare, modificare, schimbare sau incheiere a unei perioade de 

proba. 

203.4 PC MOTION – Request to take back guilty plea or set aside a guilty verdict, and dismiss the 

accusations or information.  (Made after probation has either terminated or defendant was discharged from 
probation prior to termination.) 

OTIUNEA PC 1203.4 – Cererea de retragere a pledoariei de vinovatie sau ridicarea sentintei de 

vinovatie si anularea acuzatiilor si a informatiilor. (Facuta, sau dupa terminarea probei, sau cind acuzatul a 
iesit de sub perioada de proba, inainte de terminarea ei). 

70.6 PC MOTION – Request to disqualify the assigned judge from hearing a matter. 

OTIUNEA PC 170.6- Cerere de descalificare a unui Judecator de a judeca un caz. 

95 PC MOTION – Request made by a defendant to dismiss a count of information. 

OTIUNEA PC 995 – Cererea facuta de catre un acuzat de anulare a unei anumite acuzatii. 

BANDONMENT – When a parent leaves a child without enough care, supervision, support, or parental 

contact for an excessive period of time. 

BANDON – Lasarea unui copil de catre parinte, fara ingrijire sau supraveghere, fara suport ori contact, 

pentru o perioada indelungata de timp. 

BATE  – To put an end to; to cancel out. 

NULARE - A sfirsi ceva; a anula. 

BATEMENT OF ACTION – A suit which has been set aside and ended. 

NCHEIARE A ACTIUNII - Un proces care a fost lasat deoparte si incheiat. 

BDUCTION – The offense of taking away a wife, child, or ward, by deceitful persuasion, force, or 

violence. 

APIRE – Luarea prin inselaciune , forta sau violenta a unei sotii, copil sau a unui minor care se afla in 

grija tribunalului si nu a parintilor.

ABROGATE – To repeal or cancel an old law using another law or constitutional power. 

BROGARE – A retrage sau anula o lege veche prin folosirea unei alte legi sau puteri constitutionale. 

BSTRACT – A summary of what a court or government agency does. In Traffic, document that is sent to 

the Department of Motor Vehicles (DMV) to update driving record. 

EZUMAT - Rezumatul a ceea ce face un tribunal sau o agentie de guvern. In Trafic, un document trimis 

la DMV pentru a reactualiza datele. 

BSTRACT OF JUDGEMENT- Summary of the court's final decision. Can be used as a lien if you file 

it with the county recorder. 

EZUMATUL JUDECATII - Rezumatul deciziei finale a Tribunalului. Poate fi folosit ca “lien” (vezi 

lien), daca este inregistrat la arhiva, de County. 

BSTRACT OF RECORD - Short form of the case. 

EZUMATUL CAZULUI - Rezumatul sau forma scurta a cazului. 

BUSE – (1) immoderate or improper use; (2) to do physical, sexual, or psychological harm to someone. 

BUZ – (1) Folosirea improprie sau excesiva; (2) vatamarea fizica, sexuala sau psihica a cuiva.  

BUSE OF PROCESS – Misuse of the power of the court. 

BUZ  DE  PROCES – Folosirea abuziva a puterii legislative. 

CCESSORY - A person who helps someone else commit a crime, either before or after the crime. 

OMPLICE- O persoana care participa la comiterea unei ilegalitati, inainte sau dupa comiterea ei. 

CCIDENT OR MISFORTUNE – An unintentional event; unforeseen event causing misfortune. 

CCIDENT SAU NENOROCIRE – Un eveniment neintentionat; intimplare neprevazuta care cauzeaza o 

nenorocire. 

neintentionata. 

CCOMPLICE – A person that helps someone else commit a crime. Can be on purpose or not. 

OMPLICE – O persoana care ajuta la comiterea unei infractiuni; Poate sa fie intentionata sau

2 

ACCORD – A satisfaction agreed upon between the parties in a lawsuit, which prevents further actions 
after the claim. 

CORD – Ajungerea la o intelegere satisfacatoare, intre partile implicate intr-un proces, aceasta prevenind 

continuarea procesului. 

CCORD AND SATISFACTION – Agreement by the parties to settle a claim or dispute in which the 

parties typically agree to give or accept something. 

CORD SI MULTUMIRE – O intelegere intre parti de a incheia un proces sau o disputa, (cearta sau 

neintelegere), in care, de obicei, partile accepta sa dea sau sa primeasca ceva. 

CCRUAL – The total amount of child support payments that are owed or that are late. 

----) - Suma totala a pensiei alimentare datorate. 

CCUSATION – A formal charge against a person.  

CUZATIE – Invinuirea unei persoane. 

CCUSED – The person that is charged with a crime and has to go to criminal court.  (See 

DEFENDANT). 

CUZATUL – Persoana acuzata de violarea legii si, care trebuie sa se infatiseze la Triunal. 

CKNOWLEDGEMENT – Saying, testifying, or assuring that something is true.  

ECUNOASTERE – A declara, marturisi sau confirma un adevar. 

CKOWLEDGEMENT OF SATISFACTION OF JUDGEMENT – A court form that the person who 

wins the case must fill out, sign, and file with the court when the judgment is fully paid.  If there are no 
liens, the back of the Notice of Entry of Judgment can be signed and filed with the court  (See JUDGMENT 
CREDITOR, JUDGMENT.) 

----) - Un document legal, care trebuie sa fie completat, semnat si inregistrat de Tribunal, cind procesul 
este finalizat si platit. Daca nu exista nici o datorie, documentul legal poate fi semnat pe verso, (spate), si 
inregistrat la Tribunal. 

CQUIT – To legally find the innocence of a person charged with a crime. To set free, release or 
discharge from an obligation, burden or accusation. To find a defendant not guilty in a criminal trial. 

CHITA – A gasi nevinovat  pe cineva care este acuzat de o infractiune.  A elibera , dezvinovati sau 

scoate de sub acuzatie. A gasi pe un acuzat, nevinovat intr-un proces legal.

3 

ACQUITAL – When a judge or jury finds that the person on trial is not guilty. 

CHITARE - Cind un judecator sau juratii decide ca o persoana judecata este nevinovata. 

CTION – In court, when one person sues someone else to, defend or enforce a right, stop something bad 

from happening or fix something, or punish them for a crime. 

CTIUNE – La Tribunal, cind o persoana da in judecata pe cineva, pentru a apara sau intari un drept, a 

preveni un rau, sau a pedepsi pentru o infractiune. 

CTION IN PERSONAM – Proceeding against the person for the recovery of a specific object, usually 

an item of personal property such as an automobile. 

ROCES CONTRA PERSOANEI – Procedura impotriva unei persoane pentru recuperarea unui anumit 

obiect, de obicei un bun personal, cum ar fi un automobil. 

CTION IN REM – Proceeding "against the thing" as compared to personal actions (in personam). 

Usually a proceeding where property is involved. 

ROCES CONTRA UNUI BUN – Proces contra unui “obiect “prin comparatie cu un proces contra 

persoanei. De obicei, un proces care implica un bun imobiliar, (proprietate). 

CTIVE STATUS – A case that is in court but is not settled or decided has active status. (See 

DISPOSITION, PENDING.) 

TATUT ACTIV – Un caz neincheiat, in curs de rezolvare. (Vezi DISPOZITIE, IN ASTEPTARE) 

CTUAL LOSS – This is a showing that the plaintiff or injured party has undergone some loss of property 

or other thing of value by reason of fraud, forgery, or other illegal action.  For the crime of forgery the 
existence of a specific intent to defraud is an essential element; however, there is no requirement of actual 
loss to complete the crime. 

IERDERE DE FAPT –Aceasta arata ca reclamantul sau partea vatamata, a suferit o pierdere a 

proprietatii sau a unui obiect de valoare, fie prin inselaciune, uz de fals, fie printr-o alta actiune ilegala.  
Culpa de plastografie implica existenta unei intentii de frauda, ca element esential; cu toate acestea, 
savirsirea unei infractiuni nu presupune neaparat o pierdere. 

D LITEM - Comes from Latin meaning for the "purposes of the lawsuit." For example, a guardian ad 
litem is a person appointed by the court to protect the interests of a minor or legally incompetent person in a 
lawsuit. 

D LITEM - Provine din Latina, insemnind “in scopul procesului”. De exemplu, un tutore ad litem este o 
persoana desemnata de Tribunal, sa apere interesele unui minor sau o persoana incompetenta legal, intr-un 
proces.

4 

ADD-ON – Refers to an additional matter that is added to a specific calendar at a time after the initial 
preparation of the calendar. 

DAUGIRE - Se refera la o problema aditionala care este adaugata la un calendar, dupa pregatirea initiala 

a calendarului. 

DDENDUM – A thing added or to be added. 

NEXA – Un lucru adaugat sau care va fi adaugat. 

DDICTION – A person who has become emotionally dependent on the use of a drug and the effect is an 

irresistible need to continue its use and has developed a tolerance to the drug and  requires larger stronger 
doses.  

EPENDENTA – O dependenta emotionala de folosire a unui drog care are drept efect nevoia  irezistibila 

de a continua folosirea lui si care a dezvoltat o toleranta la drog si cere doze mai mari si mai puternice. 

DDITUR – The power of a trial court to increase the amount of an award of money to one party made by 

jury verdict, as a condition of denial of motion for new trial. The defendant must consent to the increased 
money award, the plaintiff need not consent.  

DDITUR - Puterea unui Tribunal de a mari suma unei recompense banesti, date uneia din parti, printr-un  

verdict al juriului, ca o conditie a negarii unei motiuni pentru un nou proces. Piritul trebuie sa consimta la 
marirea recompensei, reclamantul nu tebuie sa consimta. 

DHESION CONTRACTS – Contract where one party has no real choice as to its terms. 

ONTRACTE DE ADEZIUNE - Contract in care una din parti nu are posibilitatea de a alege termenii. 

DJOURNMENT – To put off a court hearing until another time or place. 

MINARE – A amina un proces pina la o alta data sau un alt loc. 

DJUDICATE – When a judge hears and decides a case. 

DJUDECA – Cind un judecator audiaza si hotaraste un caz. 

DJUDICATION – The judge's decision in a case or action. 

DJUDECARE – Decizia unui judecator intr-un caz sau actiune.

5 

ADMIN PER SE – Latin meaning,“by itself, inherently.” Requires the Department of Motor Vehicles 
(DMV) to automatically suspend or cancel the driver's license of a driver whose blood alcohol content 
measures more than .08%, or who refuses to take a test to measure his/her blood alcohol level. 

DMIN PER SE - Latin insemnind  “ prin sine insusi”. Cere DMV-ului sa suspende sau sa anuleze 

automat permisul de conducere al unui conducator auto a carei alcoolemie masoara peste 0.08% sau care 
refuza testul de alcoolemie.  

DMINISTER – (1) to manage; (2) taking a drug by injection, inhalation, ingestion, or any other means, 

to the body for that person's immediate needs. 

DMINISTRA – Luarea unui medicament prin injectare, inhalare, inghitire, sau pe alte cai, pentru nevoile 

immediate ale unei persoane. 

DMINISTRATIVE  PROCEDURE – The way an executive government agency makes and enforces 

support orders without going to court. 

ROCEDURA ADMINISTRATIVA – Modul prin care o agentie guvernamentala executiva face si 

intareste ordinele pentru sprijin, fara a merge la Tribunal. 

DMINISTRATIVE  REVIEW OR  “AR” – A review of the welfare of a child in long-term foster care 
by a panel of people selected by the state Department of Health & Human Services (DHHS). The review is 
conducted at least once a year, in place of a 6-month placement hearing by the Court. The panel reviews a 
report from DHHS.  The review is open to the parents of the child, parents’ attorney and child’s attorney. 

NSPECTIE – O revizuire a situatiei copilului aflat in plasament de adoptiune, de catre un comitet selectat 
de catre Departamentul de Stat pentru Sanatate si Servicii Umane,(DHHS).  Controlul este facut cel putin o 
data pe an, in loc de o audiere de catre Curte in vederea unei plasari de 6 luni. Comitetul revizuieste un 
raport al DHHS. Inspectia este accesibila pentru parintii copilului, avocatul parintilor si avocatul copilului. 

DMINISTRATOR – 1. Man who represents the estate of a person who dies without a will. 2. A court 

official. 

DMINISTRATOR – Barbat care administreaza proprietatea unei persoane care moare fara sa lase 

testament.  O persoana cu autoritate legala. 

DMINISTRATRIX – Woman who represents the estate of a person who dies without a will. 

DMINISTRATOARE – (Vezi  ADMINISTRATOR). 

DMISSIBLE – Pertinent and proper to be considered in reaching a decision. 

DMISIBIL – Potrivit si demn de a fi luat in considerare in ajungerea la o decizie.

6 

ADMISSIBLE  EVIDENCE – Evidence that can be legally and properly be used in court. 

VIDENTA  ADMISIBILA – Dovezi, probe care pot fi folosite legal la Tribunal. 

DMISSION – Saying that certain facts are true. But not saying you are guilty. (Compare with 

ECUNOASTERE – A declara ca ceva este adevarat, dar nu a spune ca esti vinovat. (Compara cu 

CONFESSION). 

MARTURISIRE). 

DMONISH – To warn, advise, or scold. 

VERTIZA – A sfatui, a convinge, a certa. 

DMONITION – Advice or caution by the court to the jury respecting their duty or conduct as jurors, and 

the purpose for which evidence may be considered. 

VERTISMENT – Sfatuirea sau atentionarea juriului de catre Tribunal de a-si respecta sarcinile si 

conduita ca jurati si de a respecta scopul la care servesc probele. 

DMONITION TO JURORS – What the judge says to the jury about what they must do and how they 
must behave, what evidence they can use to make their decision (called "admissible" evidence), and how 
they can use that evidence to make a decision. 

FATUIREA JURATILOR – Ceea ce spune judecatorul juratilor cu privire la ce trebuie sa faca si cum 
trebuie sa se comporte, ce probe sa foloseasca pentru a lua decizia, ( numita “evidenta admisibila”), si cum 
trebuie sa foloseasca acele probe pentru luarea deciziei. 

DOPTION – The way to make the relationship between a parent and child legal when they are not 

related by blood. 

DOPTIUNE – Modul de a legaliza o relatie intre un copil si un parinte care nu sint inruditi prin singe. 

DOPTIVE ADMISSION – Action by a party that communicates agreement with the statements of 

ECUNOASTERE  ADOPTIEI – Actiune judiciara  a unei parti care-si exprima acordul cu declaratia 

another person. 

altei persoane.

7 

ADVERSARY SYSTEM -  The system of trial practice in the United States and some other countries in 
which each of the opposing (or "adversary") parties has the opportunity to present and establish opposing 
positions before the court. 

ISTEM ADVERS - Sistemul judiciar in Statele Unite si alte citeva tari in care fiecare din partile opuse, 

(sau “adversare”), are ocazia sa-si prezinte si sa-si stabileasca pozitiile opuse, inaintea Tribunalului. 

DVERSE WITNESS – A person called to testify for the other side.  

ARTORUL OPOZITIEI – O persoana chemata sa marturiseasca pentu partea opusa. 

FFIANT – A person who makes and signs an affidavit.  

FFIANT - O persoana care face sau semneaza  un “affidavit.” 

FFIDAVIT – A written statement that someone swears to under oath in front of someone that is legally 

authorized, like a judge or notary public. 

FFIDAVIT - O declaratie scrisa sub juramint, data in fata unei autoritati, cum ar fi un judecator sau un 

notar public. 

FFIRMATION – When an appellate court says that the lower court’s decision was right. 

ONFIRMARE – Cind Curtea de Apel spune ca decizia Tribunalului a fost corecta. 

FFIRMATIVE  DEFENCE – When a defendant or person responding to a civil case has a reason that 

would make him or her "not guilty" or not at fault and gives the court new evidence to prove that. The 
defense has to prove what it says (called BURDEN OF PROOF). The defense has to explain this defense in 
their ANSWER. 

ECIZIE AFIRMATIVA - Cind un pirit sau o persoana civila are o proba de nevinovatie si prezinta 

Tribunalului dovada respectiva. A pararea trebuie sa dovedeasca  ce spune, (numita GREUTATEA 
DOVEZII). Apararea trubuie sa explice aceasta proba in raspunsul ei. 

FFIRMED – In appellate courts, it means that the decision of the trial court is correct. 

ONFIRMAT – La Curtea de Apel inseamna ca decizia Tribunalului este corecta. 

FTER ACQUIRED INTENT – When the defendant did not intend to commit a crime until after the 

crime had been committed.  

UPA INTENTIE - Cind reclamatul nu a intentionat sa savirseasca o infractiune inainte de savirsirea ei. 

GENT – Someone who has authority to act for another. 

GENT – Cineva care are autoritatea de a actiona representand pe altcineva.

AGENCY – One person acts for or represents another by authority. In Traffic, the department issuing the 
citation. 

GENTIE – Autoritate abilitata sa reprezinte pe altcineva. In Trafic departamentul care elibereaza 

citatiile. 

punishment. 

GGRAVATION – Circumstances that may be considered as magnifying, or adding to, the degree of  

GRAVARE – Circumstante care sint considerate ca marind sau adaugand la gradul de pedeapsa. 

GGRAVATED ARSON –Deliberately setting fire with specific intent to cause injury or damage 

structures where defendant has been previously convicted of arson, the damage exceeds $5m, or at least 5 
residences were damaged. 

NCENDIERE  PREMEDITATA – A da foc in mod intentionat cu scopul vatamarii persoanei sau a 
proprietatii, unde reclamatul a mai fost judecat pentru incendiu, iar paguba depaseste $5m, sau cel putin 5 
case au fost distruse. 

GGRAVATED BATTERY - Unlawful use of force against another such as using a dangerous weapon. 

TAC IN FORTA – Folosirea ileagla a fortei impotriva cuiva, cum ar fi folosirea unei arme periculoase. 

GGRAVATED MAYHEM – Causing permanent disability or disfigurement with specific intent to 

cause the injury and with extreme indifference to well-being of other person. 

UTILARE – Cauzarea unei debilitati permanente sau desfigurarea cu intentia precisa de a provoca 

vatamare si cu o indiferenta extrema fata de binele celeilalte persoane. 

GGRAVATED TRESPASS – Unlawfully entering property of another with specific intent to carry out 

prior threat of serious bodily injury. 

IOLAREA GRAVA A PROPRIETATII – Intrarea ilegala pe proprietatea cuiva cu scopul de a duce la 

indeplinire o amenintare de vatamarea trupeasca a cuiva. 

GGRAVATING FACTORS – Any factors associated with the commission of a crime which increase 

the seriousness of the offense. 

ACTORI  AGRAVANTI – Orice factori asociati cu comiterea unei infractiuni care ii mareste gravitatea. 

GGREGATE TERM – The total length of imprisonment 

ERMEN - Perioada totala a intemnitarii.

9 

AGGREED STATEMENT OF FACTS – Statement of all important facts, which all the parties agree is 
true and correct, and which is submitted to a court for a decision. 

ECLARATIE ASUPRA CAREIA SE CADE DE ACORD - O declaratie in care partile sint de acord ca 

toate faptele sint adevarate si corecte, care este data la corect in vederea unei decizii. 

GREEMENT – When the people involved in a legal dispute agree about something. 

CORD – Cind persoanele implicate intr-o disputa legala cad de acord asupra unui lucru. 

ID AND ABET – to help or assist, in committing a crime. 

JUTOR – Aajuta sau incuraja comiterea unei infractiuni. 

IDER AND ABETTOR – One who has criminal intent and assists another to commit a crime. 

NSTIGATOR – Cineva care are o intentie criminala sau ajuta pe cineva sa comita o infractiune. 

LLEGE – To say, declare, or charge that something is truce even though it is not proved yet. 

RETINDE – A pretinde ca ceva e adevarat inainte de a se fi dovedit. 

LLEGED – Said to be true as described;  a person who is accused, but has not yet been tried in court. 

RESUPUS - Asa-zis adevarat dupa cum a fost descris; o persoana care a fost acuzata dar nu judecata. 

LLEGATION – A statement or claim that is made and has not been proved to be true or false. 

LEGATIE – Afirmatie nedovedita s fi adevarata sau falsa. 

LLEGED FATHER – A man who may be the father of the child. 

RESUPUS TATA - Un om care ar putea fi tatal copilului. 

LIAS – Known by another name; or means "also known as" which  A.K.A. is short for. 

LIAS - Cunoscut sub un alt nume; inseamna “cunoscut ca.” 

LIBI – A defense claim that the accused was somewhere else at the time a crime was committed. 

LIBI - Pretextul ca acuzatul se afla in alta parte cind a fost comisa infractiunea.

10 

ALIMONY – Money the court orders you to pay to a spouse or ex-spouse. (See SPOUSAL SUPPORT). 

ENSIE ALIMENTARA – Suma de bani pe care o stabileste Tribunalul ca trebuie sa fie platita 

sotiei/sotului sau fostei/fostului sotii/sot. 

LLOCUTION – Defendant's statement to try to reduce punishment. 

LOCUTIUNE – Declaratia reclamatului prin care incearca sa reduca pedeapsa. 

LTERATION, FORGERY BY – Adding, erasing, or changing a document with the specific intent to 

cause it to appear different from what it originally was intended to be to cheat another person. 

LTERARE, PLAGIERE – A adauga, sterge sau schimba un document cu scopul precis de a-l face sa 

para diferit decit cel original, in intentia de a insela o alta persoana. 

LTERNATIVE  DISPUTE  RESOLUTION (ADR) – Methods of resolving disputes without official 

court proceedings.  These methods include MEDIATION and ARBITRATION. 

EZOLVARE ALTERNATIVA A DISPUTEI - Metode de resolvare a disputelor fara sa fie necesare 

procedurile juridice. Aceste metode includ Medierea si Arbitrajul. 

MEND – To add to or change a claim that has been filed in court. 

 AMENDA – A modifica, a aduce modificari unui proces deschis la Tribunal. 

MENDMENT – A change made by correction, addition, or deletion. 

MENDAMENT – O schimbare facuta prin corectare, adaugare sau stregere. 

MICUS CURIAE (A-MI'KUS KU'RIE) - Someone that gives advice to the court about the law in a case, 

but is not part of the case. Comes from the Latin for "friend of the court." 

MICUS CURIAE  - O persoana care sfatuieste Tribunalul cu privire la aplicarea legii intr-un anumit caz, 

dar care nu este implicat in cazul respectiv. Provine din latina: Prieten al Tribunalului. 

NNOTATION – A case summary or commentary on the law cases, statutes, and rules. 

DNOTARE – Nota explicativa in procese, statute si legi. 

NNUAL REVIEW - Yearly judicial review. 

EVIZIE ANUALA - O revizuire juridica, anuala.

ANNULMENT – A legal action that says your marriage was never legally valid because of unsound mind, 
incest, bigamy, being too young to consent, fraud, force, or physical incapacity. 

NULARE – O aciune juridica prin care casatoria este declarata ilegala datorita lipsei de ratiune, 

incestului, bigamiei, sau imaturitatii de a consimti, frauda, forta, sau incapacitate fizica. 

NONYMUS – When someone's name is kept secret. 

NONIM – Cind numele cuiva este pastrat secret. 

NSWER – A statement that a defendant writes to answer a civil complaint and says what defense they 

ASPUNS – O declaratie scrisa de catre reclamat penru a replica unei plingeri civile aratind ce probe va 

will use. 

folosi apararea. 

NTICIPATORY BREACH – When a person who is to perform as set forth in a contract, clearly 

indicates to the other party that he will not or cannot perform. 

NCALCARE  ANTICIPATORIE - Cind o persoana care trebuie sa onoreze un contract stabilit, indica in 
mod clar celeilalte parti ca nu va putea onra contractul. 

PPEAL – When someone that loses at least part of a case asks a higher court (called an "APPELLATE 
COURT") to review the decision and say if it is right. This is called "to appeal" or "to take an appeal." The 
person that appeals is called the "APPELLANT." The other person is called the "APPELLEE." 

PEL – Cind cineva care pierde o parte a procesului cere la Curtea de Apel sa revizuiasca decizia si sa 
hotareasca daca aceasta a fost corecta. Aceasta se numeste “a apela” sau “a face un apel”.  Persoana care 
apeleaza se numeste ”Apelant”. Cealalta persoana se numeste “Intimat.” 

PPEARANCE – Going to court. Or a legal paper that says you will participate in the court process. 

REZENTARE – Infatisare la Tribunal.  Un document legal care sune ca trebuie sa participi intr-un 

proces. 

PPERANCE PROGRESS REPORT (APR) – A court order for a report by the Department of Health 

and Human Services (DHHS) on an issue requested by the court. 

APORT ASUPRA EVOLUTIEI JUDECATII - Un ordin al Tribunalului catre DHHS, cerind un raport cu 

referire la o problema juridica. 

PPELLANT – Someone that APPEALS a court's decision. (Compare with APPELLEE.) 

PELANT – Cineva care apeleaza o decizie a Tribunalului.

PPELLATE COURT – A court that can review how the law was used to decide a case in a lower court.

NTIMAT – Persoana care raspunde unui apel facut intr-un Tribunal Superior. 

RBITRATION – When a person that isn't involved in the case looks at the evidence, hears the 

arguments, and makes a decision. (Compare with MEDIATION.) 

RBITRARE – Cind o persoana care nu este implicata intr-un caz citareste probele, audiaza argumentele, 

si ia o decizie. (compara cu MEDIERE). 

RGUMENT – Remarks made by an attorney to a judge or jury on the facts of the case or on points of 

RGUMENT  – Remarci facute de catre un avocat inaintea judecatorului sau a juratilor, referitor la datele

RMING CLAUSE - A conduct enhancement alleging that defendant or an accomplice was 

LAUZA DE POSESIE DE ARME - care pretinde ca reclamatul sau complicele au fost inarmati. 

RRAIGN – Process where the person who is accused is brought before the court to hear the criminal 

charge(s) against him or her and to plead guilty, not guilty or no contest. 

 DA IN JUDECATA – Un proces prin care acuzatul este adus inaintea Tribunalului, pentru a i se 

prezenta acuzatiile impotriva-i, si pentru a pleda vinovat, nevinovat sau a nu contesta.

ARRAIGNMENT – When a person that is accused of committing a crime is taken to court, told about the 
charges, and asked to plead "guilty" or "not guilty." 

RIMITERE IN JUDECATA – Cind o persoana care este acuzata de o infractiune este dusa la Tribunal, 

i se prezinta acuzatiile si i se cere sa pledeze “vinovat” sau “nevinovat.” 

RREARAGE – Child support that is overdue or unpaid. 

ESTANTA – Pensie alimentara restanta sau neplatita. 

RREST – The legal capture of a person who is charged with a crime. 

REST – Capturarea legala a unei persoane care este acuzata de o infractiune. 

RREST OF JUDGEMENT – Postponing the result of a judgment already entered. 

USPENDAREA SENTINTEI – Aminarea unei judecati facute deja. 

RSON – The malicious burning of someone's own house or of someone else's house, or of someone's 

commercial or industrial property. 

NCENDIERE – Arderea malitioasa a casei personale, casei altcuiva sau a unei proprietati comerciale sau 
industriale. 

SSAULT – When someone tries or threatens to hurt someone else. Can include violence, but is not 

battery. (See BATTERY.) 

este bataie. 

SALT – Cind cineva incearca sau ameninta ca va vatama pe altcineva. Poate sa includa violenta, dar nu 

SSAULT WITH A DEADLY WEAPON – When someone tries to hurt someone and there is threat to 

do bodily harm without justification by use of a weapon like a gun or a knife. 

SALT CU O ARMA MORTALA – Cind cineva incearca sa vatame pe altcineva si exista amenitarea cu 

vatamarea corporala, fara justificare, folosind o arma, cum ar fi un pistol sau un cutit. 

SSESSMENT – Additional charges added to a case. 

AXARE – Adaugarea de noi costuri la un caz. 

SSIGNEE – A person or business that is put in the place of the original creditor, such as a collection 

agency. You can assign your JUDGMENT to another person or business. 

ANDATAR – O persoana sau un business care este plasat in locul creditorului initial, cum ar fi o agentie 

de colectii.  Poti desemna  procesul unei alte persoane sau business.

ASSIGNMENT – Choosing someone to do something.  Usually for: Cases - when the court uses a 
calendar to give (or "assign" cases to judges; Lawyers - when lawyers are chosen (or "appointed") to 
represent juveniles, conservatees or defendants; and Judges - when judges are sent (or "assigned") to 
different courts to fill in while other judges are on vacation, sick, etc., or to help with cases in a court. 

ESEMNARE – A insarcina pe cineva sa faca ceva. De obicei: Cazuri – cind un Tribunal foloseste un 
calendar pentru a da sau a transfera cazuri la judcatori; Avocati – cind avocatii sint alesi sau desemnati sa 
reprezinte persoane juvenile sau reclamati; Judecatori – cind judecatorii sint trimisi 
sau desemnati sa mearga la alte Tribunale si sa tina locul altor judecatori care sint in concediu, bolnavi, 
etc., sau sa ajute la diferite cazuri la Tribunal. 

SSIGNMENT OF SUPPORT RIGHTS – When a person who gets public assistance agrees to give the 
state any child support they get in the future.  The person gets money and other benefits from the state.  So 
the state can use part of the child support to pay for the cost of that public assistance. 

ARE A DREPTURILOR DE SUSTINERE - Cind o persoana care primeste asistenta sociala este de 
acord sa dea Statului orice pensie alimentara vor primi in viitor. Persoana primeste bani si alte beneficii de 
la Stat.  Astfel Statul va folosi parte din acesti bani pentru plata asistentei sociale. 

SSIGNMENT ORDER – A court order (made after a MOTION that says a JUDGMENT DEBTOR 
must assign certain rights to the JUDGMENT CREDITOR. Useful for payments that the judgment debtor 
would usually get, like rent from tenants, wages from the federal government, sales commissions, royalties, 
a business's accounts receivable, or installment payments on IOUs (also called "PROMISSORY NOTES" 
or JUDGMENTS).  

RDIN DE DESEMNARE – Ordin al Tribunalului, facut dupa o MOTIUNE, care spune ca persoana care 

a pierdut trebuie sa acorde anumite drepturi persoanei care a cistigat; folositoare pentru platile le-ar primi 
persoana care pierde, cum ar fi: chirii de la chiriasi, salarii de la Guvernul Federal, comisiuni pentru 
vinzari, drept de autor, conturile de credit ale unui business, sau platile regulate intr-un “IOU” 9numite de 
asemeni Note de Promisiune ) 

SSUMPTION OF RISK – A defense to a lawsuit for personal injury. The essence of the defense is that 

the plaintiff assumed the known risk of whatever dangerous condition caused the injury. 

SUMAREA  RISCULUI -  Apararea intr-un proces pentru vatamare personala. Esenta apararii este ca 

reclamantul si-a asumat riscul conditiilor care au cauzat vatamarea. 

T ISSUE – The time in a lawsuit when the complaining party has stated his or her claim and the other 

side has responded with a denial and the matter is ready to be tried. 

CAZ) IN  LITIGIU – Momentul , intr-un litigiu, cind reclamantul si-a expus plingerea si cealalta parte a 
replicat cu o negare si problema este gata sa fie judecata. 

T ISSUE MEMORANDUM – A legal paper filed in a civil case that says the case is ready to go to trial. 

EMORANDUM – Un document legal, completat intr-un caz civil, care spune ca litigiul este gata pentru 

judecare.

ATTACHMENT – (1) Document attached to court papers to give more information; (2) A way to collect

ECHESTRU -  Document atasat de actele legale pentru mai multa informatie; un mod de a obtine ce s-a

TTACHMENT FOR DEFAULTER – A process by the court for the arrest of a person other 

than a defendant. (See ATTACHMENT, BENCH WARRANT.) 

----) - Un proces, la tribunal, prin care o persoana, alta decit acuzatul, este arestata. 

TTEMPT – An effort to do an act or commit a crime. 

ENTATIVA – Un effort de a face ceva sau a comite o infractiune. 

TTEST – To witness, to affirm to be true or genuine, to certify. 

TESTA – A marturisi, a afirma ca adevarat si genuin, a certifica. 

TTESTATION – The act of witnessing something in writing, at the request of a party.

TTORNEY OF RECORD – The lawyer whose name is listed in a case record as representing someone

MPUTERNICIT – O persoana particulara (nu neaparat un avocat), autorizata de cineva sa actioneze in 
locul sau, fie intr-un scop personal, sau intr-o tranzactie oficiala.

AUDIT – When records or accounts are looked at to check that they are right and complete. 

ILANT – Cind actele contabile sint revizuite si verificate pentru a fi corecte si complete. 

UTHENTICATE – To give authority or legal authenticity to a statute, record, or other written document. 

UTENTIFICA – A da autoritate sau autenticitate legala, unui statut, act, sau orice alt document scris. 

UTO TAMPERING – The manipulation of an automobile and its parts for a specific purpose. 

UTO MANIPULAREA - Manipularea unui automobil si a partilor componente, cu un anume scop. 

UTOMATED ADMINISTRATIVE ENFORCEMENT OF INTERSTATE CASES (AEI) – Part of 
the Personal Responsibility and Work Opportunity Reconciliation Act (PRWORA) that lets states fins, put 
a lien on, and take property from people in a different state who owe money. 

UNEREA IN VIGOARE ADIMISTRATIVA A CAZURILOR INTERSTATALE - Parte a 

responsabilitatii Actului PRWORA care permite Statului sa dea amenzi, sa puna ipoteca si sa ia 
proprietatea cuiva, dintr-un alt stat, care datoreaza bani. 

UTOMATED VOICE RESPONSE SYSTEM (AVR)  – Phone system that gives information to people 

over the phone. 

ISTEM AUTOMAT- Sistem telefonic care da informatii, persoanelor. 

VERAGE ADULT PERSON – A hypothetical person who is used as an example of the entire 
community. This hypothetical person represents the interests of all, including persons religious and 
irreligious; persons of all nationalities, all adult ages and all economic, educational and social standings;  
persons with normal, healthy, average contemporary attitudes, instincts and interests concerning sex.  (in 
the context of obscenity) 

ERSOANA ADULTA TIP - Persoana ipotetica (imaginara), care este folosita spre exemplu pentru o 
intreaga comunitate. Aceasta persoana ipotetica reprezinta interesele tuturor, invluzind persoane religioase 
si nereligioase; persoane de toate nationalitatile, toate virstele adulte, si toate statutele: economic, 
educational si social; persoane cu atitudine contemporana normalasi sanatoasa, instincte si interese sexuale 
sanatoase. 

ACKLOG – All the cases that haven’t been settled or decided in the time the law says they should be. 

EZERVA – Toate cazurile care nu au fost incheiate, sau rezolvate in perioada lasata de lege. 

AD FAITH – Generally implies actual or constructive fraud, or a design to mislead or deceive another. 

EA CREDINTA – Implica, in general, o frauda de fapt sau progresiva, sau o intentie de a insela pe altul.

BAIL – A security deposit (usually money) given to release a defendant or witness from custody and to 
make sure that they go to court when they're supposed to. 

AUTIUNE – Un depozit (de obicei banesc), dat pentru eliberarea din custodie unui acuzat sau martor, 

care asigura Tribunalul ca acestia se vor prezenta la tribunal la data stabilita. 

AIL BOND – A legal paper that you buy from a bondsman and give to the court instead of bail. The 

defendant signs it and is let go. But if they don't come to court when they're supposed to, they must pay the 
amount of money on the bail bond. 

ARANTIE – O obligatiune pe care o cumperi de la un garant, si pe care o prezinti la Tribunal in loc de 
depozit. Reclamatul o semneaza si este lasat sa plece.  Daca nu se prezinta la Tribunal la timp, va trebui sa 
plateasca suma de bani pentru garantie. 

AIL BONDSMAN – Person who is responsible for paying the bond for the defendant's release from jail. 

ARANT – Persoana responsabila pentru plata garantiei, pentru eliberarea din inchisoare a reclamatului. 

AIL EXONERATION – When you get your bail back.  Or when a bail bondsman or insurance ("surety") 

company isn’t responsible for your bail anymore. 

XONERARE – Cind primesti garantia ianpoi; sau cind un garant sau o Asigurare nu mai sint 

responsabile pentru garantia ta. 

AIL FORFEITURE – A court order to let the court keep the bail deposit because the defendant didn't go 

to court when they were supposed to. 

ONFISCARE – Un ordin al Tribunalului pin care depozitul sau garantia sint pastrate, pentru ca 

reclamatul nu s-a prezentat la Tribunal, la timp. 

AILIFF – Person who is in charge of security in the court. Bailiffs are picked by sheriffs. 

UNCTIONAR  ADMINISTRATIV – O persoana insarcinata cu Securitatea la Tribunal.  Acestia sint 

selectati de sherifi. 

agreed upon services. 

consimtite. 

AILMENTS – A delivery of goods from one person to another in trust for purpose of carrying out  

ARANTARI - Transferul de bunuri de la o persoana la alta, incredintat pentru indeplinirea serviciilor 

AIL NOTICE – A legal paper from the court that says the court will make a WARRANT for arrest 

unless the defendant goes to court or pays bail. 

OTIFICARE DE AREST - Un document legal care spune ca Tribunalul va elibera un ORDIN de arest, 

daca reclamatul nu se prezinta la Tribunal sau nu-si plateste garantia.

BAIL  RECEIPT – A written statement that the court gives a defendant that says bail was paid.   

HITANTA DE GARANTIE – O hirtie scrisa pe care Tribunalul o da reclamatului  

confirmind plata garantiei. 

AIL REVIEW – A hearing established to re-evaluate the bail amount that was originally set for the 

EVIZUIREA GARANTIEI – O audiere stabilita pentru reevaluarea sumei grantiei, care a fost stabilita, 

accused. 

initial pentru acuzat. 

ALLARD MOTION – A motion for psychiatric examination of prosecutor’s witnesses (victims). 

OTIUNE DE EXAMINARE - Motiune pentru examinarea psihiatrica a marorilor acuzarii (victime). 

ANK LEVY – Way to enforce a decision against someone who owes money.  The money is taken from 

their checking or savings account at a bank, savings and loan, or credit union.  

UMA IMPUSA – Mod de a intari decizia impotriva cuiva care datoreaza bani. Banii sint luati din contul 

curent sau contul de economii, din banca, economii si imprumuturi sau uniunea de credit. 

ANKRUPT – The state or condition of a person who is unable to pay his or her debts when they are due. 

ALIMENTAT – Conditia sau starea unei persoane care nu poate sa-si plateasca datoriile, la timp. 

ANKRUPTCY – The legal way for a business or person to get help when they can't pay the money they 

owe. In bankruptcy court, they can get rid of debts by paying part of what they owe. There are special 
bankruptcy judges at these hearings. 

ALIMENT – Calea legala prin care un business sau o persoana poate obtine ajutor ca sa-si plateasca 

datoriile. In Tribunalul specializat in falimente, acestia pot sa scape de datorii, platind o parte din ce 
datoreaza. Exista judecatori specifici pentru aceste procese. 

AR – All of the lawyers qualified to practice law. For example, a state bar includes all of the lawyers 

qualified to practice law in that state. 

AROU – Toti avocatii calaficati sa practice legea. De exemplu: un barou de statii include pe toti avocatii 

calificati pentru practicarea legii, intr-un stat. 

AR EXAMINATION – A state examination that is taken in order to be admitted and licensed to practice 

XAMINAREA DE CATRE BAROU – Un Examen de Stat dat pentru a fi admis si licentiat pentru a 

law. 

practica legea.

BASE TERM – A term of imprisonment selected by the court according to the Determinate Sentencing 
Law.  

ERMEN DE SENTINTA - Un termen de puscarie selectat de Tribunal, in acord cu Legea de 

Determinare a Sentintei. 

ATTERED CHILD SYNDROME (B.C.S.) – Physical condition of a child where external or internal 

injuries result from acts committed by a parent or custodian. 

INDROM DE COPIL ABUZAT (BATUT) - Conditia fizica a unui copil, la care vatamarea interna sau 

externa este cauzata de parinte sau custodian. 

ATTERY – Illegal beating or physical violence or control of a person without their permission. 

(Compare with ASSAULT.) 

(Compara cu ASALT). 

ATAIE – Bataie ilegala sau violenta fizica sau controlarea unei persoane fara permisiunea acesteia. 

ATTERY, SPOUSAL – An offensive touching or use of force on a spouse without the spouse's consent. 

See BATTERY. 

BUZ / VIOLENTA CASNICA - O atingere ofensatoare sau folosirea fortei asupra sotiei/sotului, fara 

consimtamintul acesteia/acestuia. (Vezi BATAIE). 

EAGLE MOTION – A request to exclude any reference of the defendant’s prior conviction to the jury. 

OTIUNE BEAGLE - Cerere de a exclude orice referire la o condamnare precedenta, in fata juriului. 

EHAVIOR INTERVENTION PLAN – Plan made by a local educational agency (LEA) as part of an 
individualized education program (IEP), to change the behavior of students who harm themselves, assault 
others, or are destructive.  

LAN DE INTERVENTIE COMPORTAMENTALA - Plan facut de o agentie locala,educationala, ca 

parte a unui programde educare, individualizat, de a schimba comportamentulelvilor care se vatama 
singuri, ii asalteaza pe altii sau sint distructivi. 

ENCH – (1) the desk where a judge sits in court; (2) Judges in general, or a specific judge. 

CAUN JUDECATORESC – (1) scaunul pe care sade judecatorul, la tribunal. (2) judecatorul, in general, 

sau un anume judecator. 

ENCH CONFERENCE – A meeting either on or off the record at the judge's bench between the judge, 

counsel, and sometimes the defendant, out of the hearing of the jury. 

CAUN DE CONFERINTA - Intilnire inregistrata sau neinregistrata, la scaunul judecatoresc, intre 

judecator, avocat si uneori reclamat, fara prezenta juratilor.

ENCH TRIAL - Trial without a jury. The judge decides the case. 

  
SCAUN DE JUDECATA - Porces fara jurati. Judecatorul decide cazul. 

ENCH WARRANT – An order given by the judge (or "bench") to arrest a person who didn't do what the 

court ordered. For example, didn't go to court when they were supposed to. (See WARRANT, WRIT). 

ARANT DE  SCAUN - Ordin dat de catre judecator, de a aresta o persoana care nu a respectat ordinul 

Tribunalului. De exemplu: nu s-a prezentat la Tribunal la timp. 

ENEFICIARY – Someone who gets something from a trust.  

ENEFICIAR – Cineva care primeste ceva prin PROCURA. 

ENEFIT OF THE BARGAIN RULE – Rule which provides that a person may recover the difference 

between the actual value of the property and the value that was represented. 

ENEFICIARUL REGULII INTELEGERII - Regula care spune ca o persoana poate recupera diferenta 

dintre valoarea actuala a unei proprietati si valaoarea care a fost reprezentata. 

EQUEATH – To leave someone something in a will. 

 LASA PRIN TESTAMENT – A lasa mostenire. 

EQUESTS – What you leave someone in a will. 

ESTAMENT – Ceva lasat ca mostenire. 

EST EVIDENCE - Primary proof; the best proof available. For example, an original letter is “best 

evidence,” and a photocopy is “secondary evidence.” 

EA MAI BUNA EVIDENTA- Dovada primara; cea mai buna dovada disponibila.  De exemplu: o 

scrisoare originala este “cea mai buna dovada”, iar o fotocopie constituie dovada secundara.” 

EYOND A REASONABLE DOUBT – The burden of proof in a criminal case requiring that the jury be 

convinced that every element of a crime has been proven by the prosecution.  

INCOLO DE DUBIU REZONABIL - Greutatea evidentei intr-un proces criminal, cerind ca juriul sa fie 

convins ca fiecare element al infractiunii a fost dovedit de catre Acuzare. 

IAS – A pre-conceived opinion or a predisposition to decide a cause or an issue a certain way. 

ENDINTA – O opinie preconceputa sau predispozitia de a decide intr-un caz, intr-un anumit mod.

BIFURCATE – To try issues separately, such as guilt and criminal responsibility in a criminal proceeding 
or liability and damages in a civil action. 

IFURCARE – A judeca situatiile separat, cum ar fi vinovatia si responsabilitatea criminala intr-un proces 

criminal sao obligatii si pagube intr-un proces civil. 

IFURCATION MOTION – A request to change the order in which issues are heard at trial. 

OTIUNE DE BIFURCATIE (SEPARARE) – Cerere de schimbare a ordinei in care sint judecate 

problemele. 

ILL OF PARTICULARS – A statement of the details of the charge made against the defendant. 

OTA DETALIATA - O declaratie a acuzatiilor facute impotriva reclamatului. 

IND – To make yourself or someone else legally responsible for something. 

EGARE - A se face pe sine sau pe altcineva responsabil legal, pentru ceva. 

IND OVER – A judge's decision before a trial that says there is enough evidence for a trial. 

ECIZIE DE JUDECATA - Decizia unui judecator, inainte de judecata, care spune ca exista suficienta 

evidenta pentru judecata. 

LOOD-ALCOHOL CONTENT (BAC) - The measurement in grams of alcohol per 100 

milliliters of blood or grams of alcohol per 210 liters of breath.  

ONTINUTUL DE ALCOOL IN SINGE – Masurarea in grame a alcoolului pe 100 ml de singe sau 

grame de alcool pe 210 L de respiratie. 

LOOD TEST – Testing someone’s blood sample to: (1) see how much of a certain chemical is in the 

blood, (2) see who is the parent of a child. 
  
TEST DE SINGE – Testarea probei de singe a cuiva pentru a: (1) determina cantitatea unui anumit 
element chimic in singe, (2) determina cine esta parintele unui copil. 

ODY ATTACHMENT – A written order issued by a court directing a peace officer to take custody of 

someone and bring them before the court: 1) A witness who fails to comply with a subpoena, 2) a party 
who fails to comply with a court order in a civil action, or 3) a material witness in a criminal case. 

EGAREA TRUPULUI - Ordin scris, eliberat de Tribunal, prin care un Ofiter este trimis sa ia pe cineva 
in custodie si sa il aduca la Tribunal; (1) Un martor care nu s-a supus unei citatii, (2) o parte care refuza sa 
se supuna unui ordin al Tribunalului intr-o actiune civila, sau (3) o marturie materiala intr-un caz criminal. 

ONA FIDE – Sincere, real without fraud or deceit. Comes from the Latin "in good faith." 

ONA FIDE - Sincer, real, fara frauda sau inselaciune. Provine din latina “de buna credinta.”

BOND – A certificate or evidence of a debt.  

CTIUNE - Certificat sau evidenta a unei datorii. 

OOK (BOOKING) – What the police do when they arrest someone. Includes taking fingerprints, 

photographs, and writing down personal information about the person. 

OSAR - Ceea ce face Politia cind aresteaza pe cineva. Include luarea amprentelor, fotografii, si luarea in 

scris a informatiei personale a unei persoane. 

OOKING NUMBER – The number assigned to the criminal record that corresponds to the person's 

UMARUL DOSARULUI - Numarul atribuit registrului criminal care corespunde arestului unei 

arrest. 

persoane. 

OOKMAKING – Collecting the bets of others or making odds on future gambling events. 

ARIU SAU ACTIVITATE LEGATA DE PARIU - Colectarea de pariuri sau facerea de pronosticuri 

pentru urmatoarele jocuri de noroc.  

RADY MOTION – A motion made by defense when they believe the District Attorney has not turned 

over exculpatory and material evidence. 

OTIUNEA BRODY - Motiune facuta de Aparare cind se crede ca Avocatul de District nu a predat 

evidenta materiala si exculpatorie (de nevinovatie). 

RANDISHING A WEAPON – Showing a weapon to another person, typically the police or the victim. 

RATAREA DE ARME - A arata altei persoane arma, de obicei Politiei sau victimei. 

REACH – The breaking or violating of a law, right, obligation, or duty either by doing an act or failing to 

do an act. 

NCALCARE – Violarea sau nerespectarea legii, a dreptului, obligatiei sau indatoririi, prin a face sau a nu 
face ceva. 

REACH OF PEACE – Every person who unlawfully fights in a public place or willfully and maliciously 
disturbs another person by loud and unreasonable noise, or in a public place, says offensive words to one or 
more persons which are likely to start an immediate violent reaction.  

ERTRBAREA  LINISTII – Orice persoana care se cearta sau se bate ilegal, in public si deranjeaza o alta 

persoana prin galagie excesibila, in mod rautacios si voit, ori intr-un loc public, sau adreseaza cuvinte 
ofensatoare uneia sau mai multor persoane, care ar putea sa determine o reactie violenta, imediata.

CALIFORNIA RULES OF COURT – The rules for practices and procedures in California’s state courts. 

EGULI DE TRIBUNAL IN CALIFORNIA – Reguli pentru proceduri si practici in tribunalele de stat 

ale Californiei. 

ALJIC – CALIFORNIA JURY INSTRUCTIONS, CRIMINAL. 

ALLING THE DOCKET - The public calling of the docket or list of causes at the beginning of court, 

for setting a time for trial or entering orders. 

TRIGAREA  ROLULUI – Strigarea publica a rolului sau listei de procese la inceputul sesiunii, pentru a 

desemna ora judecatii sau nitrarea ordinelor. 

APACITY – The person with the ability to perform under his or her will. 

APACITATE – Persoana cu abilitatea de se manifesta in de acord cu propria-i vointa. 

APITAL CASE - A criminal case where the defendant can get the death penalty. 

AZ CAPITAL – Caz criminal in care reclamatul poate fi condamnat la moarte. 

APITAL CRIME - A crime punishable by death. 

RIMA CAPITALA – O crima care se poate pedepsi cu moartea. 

APITAL OFFENSE – A crime that you can get the death penalty for committing. 

FENSA CAPITALA – Crima care poate fi pedepsita cu moartea. 

APITAL PUNISHMENT - Punishment by death.  (See DEATH PENALTY.) 

EDEAPSA CAPITALA – Pedeapsa cu moartea. 

APTION - What is written at the top of all papers (called "pleadings") given to the court. It says things 

like case name, court, and case number. 

ITLU – Ceea ce este scris pe partea de sus a oricarei hirtii (numite “pledoarii”) date tribunalului 

reprezentind numele cazului, Trbunalul, numarul cazului. 

ARJACKING – Taking a motor vehicle that belongs to someone else against his will, by means of force 

UAREA ILEGALA/ FARA ACORD A MASINII - Luarea vehiculului cuiva, impotriva vointei lor, 

or fear.  

prin folosirea fortei sau infricosarii.

ASE – A lawsuit. Or a complaint filed in criminal, traffic, or civil court. 

AZ – Un proces legal. O plingere adusa infata unui tribunal criminal, de trafic, sau civil. 

ASE FILE – The folder that has official court papers for a case.  

OSARUL UNUI CAZ – Un dosar care contine toate documentele legale ale unui caz. 

ASEFLOW MANAGEMENT – How a case is managed from the first paper filed to the final decision. 

DMINISTRAREA DECURGERII CAZULUI - Administrarea unui caz incepind cu primul document 

prezentat si pina la ultima decizie luata. 

ASE ID – Identification number given to case by the court. 

UMARUL DE IDENTIFICARE A CAZULUI - Numarul de identificare dat cazului d catre tribunal. 

ASE LAW – Law made by earlier decisions in similar cases. 

URISPRUDENTA – Lege elaborata prin decizii anterioare, in cazuri similare. 

ASELOAD – The number of cases a judge has in a specific time. 

ARCINA DE CAZURI - Numarul de cazuri pe care le are un judecator intr-un interval de timp. 

ASE NUMBER – The number that identifies a case. This number is on all papers filed in the case. Also 

called "case ID." Also called DOCKET NUMBER. 

UMARUL DE CAZ – Numarul care identifica un caz. Acest numar se gaseste pe fiecare document 

apartinind cazului. Se numeste deasemeni  “case ID.” 

AUSATION – The act which causes something else to happen. 

RICINUIRE – Un act care atrage dupa sine o intimplare. 

AUSE – A lawsuit, litigation, or action.  

AZ – Un proces, litigiu sau actiune. 

AUSE OF ACTION – The charges that make up the case or lawsuit. (See COUNTS). 

OIVUL  ACTIUNII – Acuzatiile care duc la un caz sau un proces.

CAUSTIC CHEMICALS – Corrosive acid or flammable substance. 

UBSTANTE ACIDE – Acid coroziv sau subtanta inflamabila. 

AUTIONARY INSTRUCTIONS – When the judge tells the jury to consider certain evidence only for a 

specific purpose.  

NSTRUCTIUNI   PREVENTIVE – Cind un judecator cere juriului sa considere anumite probe, cu un 
scop exclusiv. 

AVEAT – A warning; a note of caution. 

VERTIZARE - Avertizare, nota de prevenire. 

AVEAT EMPTOR - A theory that says you buy things at your own risk. Comes from the Latin for "let 

the buyer beware."  

----) - Teorie care spune ca iti cumperi lucruri pe propriul risc. Provine din latina: “cumparatorul sa fie 
atent.” 

EASE AND DESIST ORDER - An order of an administrative agency or court prohibiting a person or 

business from doing something. 

----) - Ordin al unei agentii administrative sau al unui tribunal care interzice unei persoane de a face ceva. 

ERTIFICATE OF PROBABLE CAUSE - An order signed by the court granting a defendant the right 

to appeal from a plea of guilty. 

----) - Ordin semnat de Tribunal care permite unui reclamat sa faca recurs la incriminare. 

ERTIFICATION - A judge's order to move a criminal case to another court in a different county. 

----) - Ordinul unui judecator de a muta un caz penal la un alt tribunal sau intr-un alt district. 

ERTIFIED - Saying that something is true or an exact reproduction. 

ERTIFICAT – A confirma ceva ca adevarat sau ca reproducere exacta. 

ERTIFIED COPY - An official copy of a paper from a case file that is marked as being true, complete, 

and a real copy of the original legal case. 

OPIE AUTENTIFICATA – Copie oficiala a unui document, intr-un proces, care se confirma a fi 

adevarata, completa si o copie reala a procesului legal original.

CERTIORI - Appeal to U.S. Supreme Court. 

----) - Apel facut la TRIBUNALUL  SUPREM AL S.U.A. 

HAIN OF CUSTODY - A method to track the whereabouts of evidence from the moment it is received 

in custody until it is offered in court. 

----) - Metoda de supraveghere a evidentei din momentul in care este primita in custodie si pina cind este 
oferita la judecata. 
 
 
 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

HALLENGE - Someone's right to object to or fight something in a legal case. 

ECUZARE – Dreptul cuiva de a obiecta sau contesta ceva, intr-un proces legal. 

HALLENGE FOR CAUSE - Reasons that a lawyer gives for removing a juror or judge from a case. 

(Compare with PEREMPTORY CHALLENGE.) 

----) - Motivele invocate de un avocat pentru inlaturarea unui jurat sau a unui judecator, dintr-un proces 
legal. 

HALLENGE TO THE ARRAY - Questioning the qualifications of an entire jury panel, usually on the 

ground of partiality or some fault in the process of summoning the panel. 

ONTESTAREA LISTEI JURATILOR – Contestarea calitatii de jurati, bazata pe partialitate sau o 

greseala facuta in procesul de citare a listei de jurati.   

HAMBERS - A judge's private office.  

ABINETUL JUDECATORULUI – Biroul personal al judecatorului. 

HANGE OF VENUE - When a civil or criminal case is moved from one court jurisdiction to another. 

(See VENUE). 

CHIMBAREA JURISDICTIEI – Transferul unui proces,criminal sau civil, de sub jurisdictia unui 

tribunal sub jurisdictia altui tribunal. 

HARACTER EVIDENCE - Evidence pertaining to whether a criminal defendant is a good or bad 

person.  

ARACTER EVIDENT – Evidenta privitoare la caracterul bun sau rau, al unui reclamat. 

HARGE - In criminal law, each thing the defendant is accused of. (See COUNT). 

CUZATIE – In Codul Penal, fiecare lucru de care e acuzat reclamatul.

HARGE TO THE JURY - The judge's instructions to the jury concerning the law that applies to the

ISCURS ADRESAT JURATILOR – Insructiuni date juriului de catre judecator, referitoare la legea

HARGING DOCUMENT - A written accusation saying a defendant has committed an offense. Includes 

a citation, an indictment, information, and statement of charges. 

OCUMENT DE ACUZARE – Orise acuzatie declarind ca reclamatul a comis un delict. Include o 

citatie, acuzatie, informatie si o declatratie a acuzatilor. 

HATTEL – A piece of personal property. 

VERE – O piesa din proprietatea personala. 

HIEF JUDGE - Presiding or Administrative Judge in a court. 

RESEDINTELE TRIBUNALULUI – Judecatorul administrativ sau care prezideaza Tribunalul. 

HILD ABUSE - Hurting a child physically, sexually or emotionally. 

BUZUL UNUI COPIL – Vatamareafizica, sexuala sau emotionala a unui copil. 

HILD ABDUCTION – The offense of taking away a child by deceit and persuasion, or by violence. 

APIREA NI COPIL – Ofensa de luare a unui copil fie prin metode de convingere, fie prin violenta. 

HILD MOLESTATION - Any form of indecent or sexual activity on, involving, or surrounding a child 

under the age of 18. 

OLESTAREA UNUI COPIL – Orice forma de activitate sexuala indecenta, asupra unui copil, 

implicindu-l pe copil sau facuta in preajma unui copil, sub virsta de 18 ani. 

HILD PORNOGRAPHY - Any obscene material that depicts a person under the age of 18 years 

personally engaging in or personally simulating sexual conduct. 

ORNOGRAFIE  INFANTILA – Orice material obscen care descrie o persoana sub virsta de 18 ani, 

angajindu-se in sau simulind un act sexual.

CHILD PROCUREMENT - Intentionally giving, transporting, providing, or making available or offering 
to give, transport, provide, or make available a child under the age of 16 for the purpose of any lewd or 
lascivious act.  Also causing, inducing, or persuading a child under the age of 16 to engage in any lewd or 
lascivious act with another person.   

ROXENETISM – Ada , a transporta, a furniza sau a pune la dispozitie; a oferi sa dai, sa transporti, sa 
furniza, sau sa pune la dispozitie un copil sub virsta de 16 ani, in scopul unui act lascivios sau de desfrinare. 

HILD SUPPORT - Money paid by a parent to help support a child or children. 

ENSIE ALIMENATARA – Suma de bani platita de un parinte pentru suportul unui copil sau al mai 

multora. 

HILD SUPPORT ENFORCEMENT (CSE) AGENCY  - Agency that exists in every state to find 

parents that don’t have custody. (called "noncustodial parents," or "NCPs"). Or to find a person assumed to 
be the father of the child (“Putative father” or "PF").  Also, makes, enforces, and changes child support.  
Collects and gives out child support money.  

GENTIE DE APLICARE A INTRETINERII COPILULUI – Agentie care se gaseste in fiecare Stat si 

care gaseste parinti care nu au custodie, (numiti parinti noncustodiali). A gasio persoana  presupusa  a fi 
tatal copilului. De asemeni intareste si face schimbari in intrtinerea copilului. Colecteaza si trimite banii 
pentru intretinere. 

IRCUMSTANTIAL EVIDENCE - All evidence that is indirect. Testimony not based on actual personal 

knowledge or observation of the facts in dispute. 

----) - Toate dovezile indirecte. Marturie care nu este bazata pe cunoastere sau observarea personala a 
faptelor, disputate. 

ITATION - A COURT ORDER or SUMMONS that tells a defendant what the charges are. Also tells the 

defendant to go to court and/or post bail. 

ITATIE – Un ordin legal sau somatie care-l informeaza pe reclamat despre acuzatiile aduse. De asemeni, 

il informeaz pe reclamat sa mearga la tribunal sau sa plateasca garantie (cautiune). 

ITED – When a defendant is not in custody, but has signed a ticket promising to go to court on a certain 

ITAT – Cind un reclamat nu se afla in custodie, dar a semnat un tichet promitind ca va merge la tribunal, 

day.  

la o anumita data. 

IVIL ACTION - Noncriminal case in which one private individual or business sues another to protect, 

enforce private or civil rights. 

ROCES CIVIL – Proces necriminal in care o pessoana pariculara sau un business da in judecata pe 

altcineva pentru a se proteja, sau sa intareasca drepturi private sau civile.

CIVIL CASE - A lawsuit to get property back, to force someone to complete a contract, or to protect 
someone's civil rights. 

ROCES CIVIL – Actiune juridica pentru returnarea proprietatii, silirea cuiva sa respecte un contract sau 

protejarea drepturilor civile ale cuiva. 

IVIL JURISDICTION – A court’s right or power to hear noncriminal civil cases.  

URISDICTIE CIVILA – Dreptul sau puterea unui tribunal de a audia cazuri nepenal. 

IVIL PROCEDURE - The rules and process by which a civil case is tried and appealed, including the 

preparations for trial, the rules of evidence and trial conduct, and the procedure for pursuing appeals. 

ROCEDURA CIVILA – Regulile si procedurile prin care un proces civil este judecat si apelat, incluzind 

pregatirilepentru judecata, regulile de administrare a probelor si desfasurarea dezbaterii, si procedura de 
apelare. 

IVIL PROCESS – Court papers that tell the people in a civil case that it has started.  Or papers that try to 

force the court to reach a judgment. 

ROCES CIVIL – Document legal care instiinteaza persoana implicata intr-un proces civil despr

LAIM - The statement of a right to money or property. 

EVENDICARE – Declaratie a dreptului la bani sau proprietate. 

LAIM OF EXEMPTION – A court paper filed by the JUDGMENT DEBTOR that lists each piece of 

property that the judgment debtor claims is an exempt asset under certain provisions of the law and, 
therefore, can’t be taken to pay the JUDGMENT. 

----) - Document legal prezentat de DEBITOR care enumera bunurile care prin anumite dispozitii ale legii, 
nu pot fi ipotecate. 

LAIM SPLITTING – When you split up a civil claim and file two lawsuits to stay below the limit of 

how much money you can ask for.  Not allowed in most cases. 

----) - Separarea unei petitii civile in doua actiuni jurdice, pentru a ramine sub limita sumei pe care o poti 
cere. In cele mai multe procese nu este admis.

31 

CLASS ACTION - A lawsuit brought by one or more persons on behalf of a larger group. 

CTIUNE DE MASA -  Actiune juridica adusa de mai multe persoane, in numele unui grup extins. 

LEAR AND CONVINCING EVIDENCE - Standard of proof commonly used in civil lawsuits and in 
regulatory agency cases. It governs the amount of proof that must be offered in order for the plaintiff to win 
the case. 

VIDENTA INDUBITABILA – Tipul de evidenta folosit in mod comun in procesele civile si factorul de 

reglementare a practicilor judecatoresti. Reglementeaza numarul de probe care trebui sa fie prezentate, 
pentru ca reclamantul sa cistige procesul. 

LEMENCY OR EXECUTIVE CLEMENCY - Act of grace or mercy by the president or governor to 
ease the consequences of a criminal act, accusation, or conviction. It may take the form of commutation or 
pardon. 

LEMENTA - Act de gratiere sau clementa facut de presedinte sau guvernator pentru a diminua 

consecintele unui act penal, acuzatie sau condamnare. Poate lua forma de comutare sau iertare. 

LERICAL ERROR - An unintentional mistake, in writing, which may be made by clerk, counsel, or 

court. (See NUNC PRO TUNC.) 

ROARE SECRETARIALA – Greseala neintentionata, in scris, care poate fi facuta de functionar, de 

avocat sau de tribunal. (Vezi NUNC PRO TUNC.)  

LERK - Officer of the court who files pleadings, motions, judgments, etc., issues process, and keeps 

records of court proceedings. 

UNCTIONAR – Ofiter al Tribunalului care inregisteaza dezbateri, motiuni, judecati, etc., redacteaza 

procese si tine evidenta procedurilor tribunalului. 

LERK’S TRANSCRIPT - Those pleadings, minute orders, affidavits, written opinions of the Court, trial 

exhibits, etc., designated by the attorneys which have been filed during the course of the litigation process 
are put together with the appeal documents and collectively form the Clerk’s Transcript. 
  
(----) - Pledoariile, minuturile depozitiile, opiniile scrise ale tribunalului, probe materiale ale judecatii, etc., 
consemnate de avocati si care au fost inregistrate in cursul desfasurarii procesului, sunt puse impreuna cu 
documentele de apel si impreuna formeaza . 

LOSING ARGUMENT - Counsel's final statement to the judge/and or jury after all parties have 

concluded their presentation of evidence. 

RGUMENTUL CONCLUSIV – Cuvintul final al avocatului, dupa ce toate partile si-au incheiat 

prezentarea probelor.

CODE - The law created by statutes. For example, the California Code of Civil Procedure, California Civil 
Code, California Vehicle Code, California Penal Code, and California Health and Safety Code.  

OD – Legea creata prin statute. De exemplu: Codul de Procedura Civla al Californiei, Codul Civl al 
Californiei, Codul de vehicole al Californiei, Codul Penal al Californiei si Codul Sanatatii si Sigurantei 
californiei. 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

ODE OF PROFESSIONAL RESPONSIBILITY - The rules of conduct that govern the legal 

profession. The Code contains general ethical guidelines and specific rules written by the American Bar 
Association. 

ODUL DE ETICA PROFESIONALA – Reguli de conduita in institutia legislativa. Codul contine 

indrumari de etica generala si reguli specifice elaborate de Asociatia Baroului American. 

O-DEFENDANT - In a criminal case, an individual charged with involvement in the same crime as 

another. 

O-ACUZAT – Un individ acuzat de implicarea in aceeasi infractiune cu altcineva, intr-un proces penal. 

ODICIL (kod'i-sil) - A legal paper that adds to or changes a will. 

----) - Document legal care adauga la, sau schimba un testament.  

OERCION – Compulsion; constraint; compelling by force or arms or threat. 

OERCITIUNE – Compulsie; constringere; fortarea inarmata sau prin amenintare. 

ONFIDENTIAL RECORD – Information in a court case that is not available to the public. 

NFORMATIE CONFIDENTIALA – Informatie, intr-un proces, care nu este accesibila publicului. 

ONFIDENTIALITY – Treated as private and not for publication. 

ONFIDENTIALITATE – De natura privata, nu pentru acces public. 

ONFISCATE - To seize or take private property for public use (the police took the weapon). 

ONFISCA – Luarea proprietatii cuiva pentru folos public. (Politia a luat arma). 

ONFLICT OF INTEREST - When you have two different interests at the same time.  For example, a 

lawyer who represents two sides at the same time can't be fair. 

ONFLICT DE INTERESE – Cind ai doua interese diferite deodata. De exemplu: un avocat care 

reprezinta doua parti, in acelasi timp, nu poate fi drept.

CONFORM COPIES - To make copies identical to an original; e.g., copies with duplicate signatures, 
duplicate dates. 

OPII  IDENTICE  –  A  face  copii  identice  cu  originalul;  ex:  copii  cu  semnatura  in  duplicat,  date  in 

duplicat. 

ONFRONTATION RIGHT – Defendant’s right to be face-to-face with the witnesses against him or her.  

It generally includes the right to ask questions and object, and to have witnesses testify in person.  

REPT DE CONFRUNTARE – Dreptul acuzatului de a sta fata in fata cu martorul acuzarii.  In general, 

include dreptul de a pune intrebarisi a obiecta si a avea martorii in persoana. 

ONSANGUINITY – COLLATERAL - The relationship that exists between persons who have the same 

ancestors, but who do not descend, or ascend, one from the other; as between uncle and nephew. 

OSANGUINITATE COLATERALA – relatia care exista intrepersoane care au aceeasi ascendenti, dar 

care nu asced sau nu descind unul dintr-altul; ex:unchi si nepot. 

ONSANGUINITY – LINEAL - The relationship that exists persons of whom one is descended in a 
direct line from the other, as between son, father, grandfather, and so upwards in the direct ascending line; 
or between son, grandson, great-grandson, and so downwards in the direct descending line. 

OSANGUINITATE  LINEARA – Relatia care exista intre persoane, in care unul descinde in linie 
directa din celalat, ca si intre fiu, tata, bunic, si asa mai departe in linie ascendenta; sau intre fiu, nepot, 
stranepot, si asa mai departe, in linie direct descendenta. 

ONSECUTIVE SENTENCES - Successive sentences, one beginning at the end of another, imposed 

against a person convicted of two or more violations. 

ENTINTE  SUCCESIVE – Sentinte care incep una la sfirsitul celeilalte, impuse unei persoane 

condamnata de una sau mai multe violari. 

ONSERVATEE - Someone who can't take care of themselves and has a caretaker (called the 

"CONSERVATOR") who the court picked. 

----) - Cineva care nu se poate ingriji pe sine si are ingrijitor, ales de Tribunal. 

ONSERVATOR - Someone picked by the court to either take care of someone who can't take care of 

themselves (called a "CONSERVATEE") or take care of that person's property , or both. 

----) - Cineva ales de Tribunal, fie sa ingrijeasca pe cineva incapabil sa se ingrijeasca pe sine, fie sa 
ingrijeasca de proprietatea acestuia.

CONSERVATORSHIP - A court proceeding where a judge picks someone (a conservator) to take care of 
an adult's personal needs and/or his or her finances.  For minors, see GUARDIANSHIP.  

----)  -  Procedura  juridica  in  care  judecatorul  alege  pe  cineva  sa  aiba  grija  de  nevoile  personale  ale  unui 
adult, sau de finantele lui/ei. Pentru minori, vezi TUTORE. 

ONSENT – A written agreement to obey a decision or deal.   

ONSIMTAMINT – Un angajament scris de a respecta o decizie sau o intelegere. 

ONSIDERATION - The cause, price, or impelling influence which makes a party enter into a contract. 

ONSIDERARE – Cauza, pretul sau influenta determinanta care face ca o parte sa intre intr-un contract. 

ONSOLIDATION OF ACTIONS – When at least two cases that involve the same people are grouped 

ONSOLIDARE  DE  ACTIUNI – Cind cel putin doua cazuri care implica aceiasi oaemni, sint grupate 

together. 

impreuna. 

ONSORTIUM, LOSS OF – Unable to have a sexual relationship between a husband and a wife. 

IERDEREA CONSORTIULUI – Incapacitatea de a avea relatii sexuale intre sot si sotie. 

ONSPIRACY – Where two or more persons intentionally agree to commit crime and do an act towards 

committing the crime. 

ONSPIRATIE – Cind doua sau mai multe persoane intentioneaza, in de acord, sa comita o infractiune, 

sau sa comita un act in scopul acesta. 

ONSTRUCTIVE POSSESSION - Where a person does not actually possess a thing, but knowingly has 

control over it. 

----) - Cind o persoana nu poseda un lucru dar are control, in mod constient, asupra lui. 

ONSTITUTION – The central law of our country that sets up the creation, character, and organization of 

its power and how that power is exercised. The rule, principles, descriptions of the government’s power, 
and the main rights that the people of a country or state have.  

ONSTITUTIE – Legea centrala a tarii noaster care stabileste creerea, caracterul, si organizarea puterii ei, 

si cum este exercitata puterea. Legea, principiile, descrierea puterii guvernului, si dreprurile principale pe 
care le are populatia unei tari sau stat.

CONSTITUTIONAL RIGHT - A right guaranteed by the U. S. Constitution, interpreted by the federal 
courts; also, a right guaranteed by some other constitution (such as a state constitution). 

REPT CONSTITUTIONAL – Drept garantat de catre Constitutia  Statelor Unite, interpretate de curtile 

federale, de asemeni, drept garantat printr-o alta constitutie (ex: constitutia statului). 

ONTEMNOR - One who has committed contempt of court. 

----) - Cineva care sfideaza curtea. 

ONTEMPORARY COMMUNITY STANDARD – What is, objectively acceptable to the community 

as a whole.  Ascertainment of the standard must be based upon an objective determination of what is 
unacceptable to the community as a whole.  Your own personal, social, or moral views on the material 
involved in the case may not be considered. 

----) - Ceea ce ese in mod obiectiv acceptat de comunitate in ansamblu. Stabilirea standardului trebuie sa 
fie bazat pe o o determinare obiectiva a ce este inacceptabil, in nasamblu de catre comunitate. Vederile 
personale, sociale, sau morale asupra materialului implicat, s-ar putea sa nu fie cosiderat. 

ONTEMPT (OF COURT) - Disobeying a court order. Punishment can be a fine or jail. 

FIDARE – Ignorarea ordinului tribunalului. Pedeapsa poate fi amenda sau inchisoarea. 

ONTINUANCE - Putting off a court case to a later date. (See ADJOURNMENT). 

MINARE – Reprogramarea unui proces pentru o data viitoare. 

ONTINUING EXCLUSIVE JURISDICTION  – Theory that only one support order should be valid 
between the same people at a time.  And when a court hears a child support case, it can add to and change 
that order.  The court of continuing exclusive jurisdiction has control over a support case until another court 
takes it away. This is defined in the Uniform Interstate Family Support Act (UIFSA). 

----) - Teoria ca numai un singur ordin de suport ar trebui sa fie valabil intre aceleasi persoane, la un 
moment dat. Intr-un proces pentru pensia alimentara a copilului, tribunalul poate sa adauge sau sa schimbe 
acel ordin. Jurisdictia permanenta si exclusiva a tribunalului are control asupra procesului de suport pina 
cind este luat de un alt tribunal. Acesta este definit in UIFSA. 

ONTRACT - (1) an agreement between two or more people to do or not to do a particular thing; (2) an 

agreement between two or more people that makes, changes, or ends a legal relationship. 

----) - (1) Intelegerea dintre doua sau mai multe persoane de a face sau a nu face ceva anume; (2) 
intelegere dintre doua sau mai multe persoane care face, schimba sau incheie o relatie legala.

CONTRIBUTORY NEGLIGENCE - A legal doctrine that says if the plaintiff in a civil action for 
negligence also was negligent, in any way, he or she cannot recover damages from the defendant for the 
defendant's negligence.  

EGLIJENTA CONTRIBUTORIE – Doctrina legala care intr-o actiune civila  de neglijenta, spune ca 
daca reclamantul a fost de asemeni neglijent, in orice masura, el sau ea nu poate recupera pagubele de la 
reclamat, datorate neglijentei reclamatului. 

ONTROLLED SUBSTANCES – Any drug identified by law whose availability is restricted.  Unless 
otherwise specified, a drug, substance, or immediate precursor which is listed in any schedule in Health & 
Safety Code sections 11054, 11055, 11056, 11057 or 11058.   

----) - Orice medicament identificat prin lege, al carei accesibilitate este limitata. Daca nu este mentionat 
altfel, un medicament, substanta sau precursor imediat care este enumerat pe orice programa in Codul 
Sanatatii si Sigurantei, sectiile:11054, 11055, 11056, 11057 or 11058. 

ONVERSION - The wrongful assumption of ownership over the goods or personal property belonging to 

another. 

ONVERTIRE – Insusirea ilegala a bunurilor sau proprietatii personale apartinind altcuiva. 

ONVEY – (1) to give the title to property to someone else.  (2) to make known or communicate. 

RANSFERA – (1) A da dreptul de proprietate altcuiva. (2) a transmite, a comunica. 

ONVICT - (1) A person who has been found guilty of a crime and is serving a sentence for that crime; a 

prison inmate. (2) To find a person guilty of an offense by either a trial or a plea of guilty. 

ONDAMNAT – (1) Persoana care a fost gasita vinovata de o infractiune, si serveste o sentinta pentru 
infractiunea respectiva; un intemnitat. (2) A gasi o persoana, vinovata de o ofensa fie prin judecare sau 
declaratie de vinovatie. 

ONVICTION - When a judge or jury finds a criminal defendant guilty.  

ONDAMNARE – Cind un judecator sau un corp de jurati il gaseste pe acuzat, vinovat. 

ORONER - Public official charged to inquire into the causes and circumstances of any death which 

occurs through violence or suddenly (suspicious causes). 

ROCUROR – Autoritate publica insarcinata sa ancheteze cauzele si circumstantele unui deces subit sau 

prin violenta. (Cauze suspecte). 

ORPORATION - A group of persons who get a charter granting them as a body certain legal powers, 

rights, privileges, and liabilities as an individual.  

ORPORATIE – Un grup de persoane carora li se garanteaza puteri legale ca si corp, drepturi, privilegii

CORPUS DELECTI - Body of the crime. The objective proof that a crime has been committed. It 
sometimes refers to the body of the victim of a homicide or to the charred remains of a burned house, but 
the term has a broader meaning. For the state to introduce a confession or to convict the accused, it must 
prove the occurrence of a specific injury or loss and a criminal act was the source of that particular injury 
or loss. 

ORP DELICT –  Obiectul crimei. Dovada obiectiva ca o infractiune a fost comisa.  Uneori se refera la 

trupul victimei unei omucideri, sau la ramasitele carbonizate ale unei case arse, dar termenul are o 
insemnatate mai larga. Pentru ca statul sa introduca o marturie sau sa condamne acuzatul, trebuie sa 
dovedeasca faptul ca o anume vatamare sau pierdere si un act cirminal, a fost sursa acelei vatamari sau 
pierderi. 

ORROBORATE - To support with evidence or authority; make more certain. 

OROBORA – A sustine prin evidenta sau autoritate; a stabili cu certitudine. 

ORROBORATING EVIDENCE - Supplementary evidence that tends to strengthen or confirm the 

VIDENTA COROBORANTA – Evidenta suplimentara care tinde sa intareasca sau sa confirme evidenta 

initial evidence. 

initiala. 

ORROBORATION - Confirmation or support of a witness' statement or other fact. 

OROBORARE – Confirmarea suportului declaratiei unui martor sau alt fapt. 

ORRUPTLY - Dishonestly. 

ORUPT – Necinstit. 

OSTS - (1) Fees and charges that a party pays to file and present a court case or to enforce a judgment; 

(2) money won in a civil suit to pay for expenses. 

HELTUIELI  DE  JUDECATA – (1) Taxe pe care le plateste o persoana pentru a deschide un proces 

legal sau a impune o sentinta; (2) bani cistigati intr-un proces civil pentru a plati cheltuielile. 

OUNSEL - One or more lawyers who represent a client. Also, legal advice. (See ATTORNEY). 

VOCAT – Unul sau mai multi avocati care reprezinta un client.  De asemeni sfat legal. 

OUNSEL TABLE - The physical location where the defense and prosecuting parties are seated during 

ASA AVOCATILOR – Locul propriu-zis unde sint asezate partea acuzarii si cea a apararii, in timpul 

the trial. 

procesului.
